SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CreatedDate], [p].[Img], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [t].[ProductId], [t].[AuthorId], [t].[Id], [t].[CreatedDate], [t].[FullName], [t].[Img]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[ProductId], [p0].[AuthorId], [a].[Id], [a].[CreatedDate], [a].[FullName], [a].[Img]
    FROM [ProductAuthors] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Authors] AS [a] ON [p0].[AuthorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [t].[ProductId], [t].[AuthorId]

FROM [Products] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[ProductId], [p0].[AuthorId], [a].[Id], [a].[CreatedDate], [a].[FullName], [a].[Img]
    FROM [ProductAuthors] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Authors] AS [a] ON [p0].[AuthorId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
